๏บู๏บดูููููููููููููู๏ปขู ๏บ๏ป๏ป๏ปชู ๏บ๏ป๏บฎูู๏บฃู๏ปคู๏ปฆู ู๏บ๏ป๏บฎูู๏บฃู๏ปดูููููู๏ปข

๐ INTISARI KHUTBAH JUMAAT JDT ๐
๐ DATE: 29 SYAABAN 1443H/ 1 APRIL 2022

๐ TITLE: THE EXPECTED RAMADHAN

The words of Allah SWT in Surah Al Baqarah verse 185 which means: the difference between right and wrong. So whoever of you witnesses the month of Ramadan (or knows it), then let him fast that month. "

๐ 1. Be pious to Allah SWT.

๐ 2. In a few days we will celebrate the arrival of the month of Ramadan which is full of glory, mercy and blessings. The month in which the Qurโan was revealed and promised with mercy at the beginning of the coming, followed by the forgiveness of sins in the middle and liberation from the fire of hell at the end. And the night of Lailatul Qadar.

๐ 3. The month of Ramadan is the best time for us to educate ourselves towards goodness for which we are not only obliged to fast and control lust, but we are even required to increase our deeds of worship. For the servants of Allah who truly live the month of Ramadan, the reward will be doubled, prayers will be granted, sins will be forgiven, the gates of heaven will be opened wide and the gates of hell will be closed and the devil will be shackled.

๐ 4. We need to prepare ourselves to celebrate the month of Ramadan and strive to live it with practices that can bring us closer to Allah SAW. Pray for a long life and the best health to worship during the month of Ramadan. Doing physical preparation because a healthy limb will make it easier for a person to worship.
 
๐ 5. Spiritual preparation is also necessary to increase our faith in Allah SAW. We must always be submissive and obedient to all his commands and be confident of the rewards and benefits that will be obtained throughout the month of Ramadan.

๐ 6. We also need to learn and review the knowledge about fasting to ensure that the worship we do is accepted by Allah SAW and in turn give a good effect to ourselves. Let us be determined to forsake sins and bad deeds by repenting of all sins because Ramadan is the month of purification of the soul and removal of sins.

๐ 7. Financial preparation should also be taken into account because it is highly encouraged to do the practice of giving alms jariah such as the practice of feeding people who are fasting.

๐ 8. In conclusion, in conjunction with the arrival of Ramadan, let us take advantage and take the opportunity and try to live the month of Ramadan by doing as many acts of worship. Make Ramadhan this time as a month for us to double our deeds to obtain great rewards and rewards in the sight of Allah SWT. May this month of Ramadan bring a great change in us to become pious servants in the sight of Allah SAW.

Waallahua'lam.

#Provided by Sermon & Tafsir Unit, PMS-JAINJ
[01/04/2022, 7:17:38โฏAM] ูุญูุฏ ุจุงุฏุจูุงู UTM: *ุงูุณูููุงููู ุนููููููููู ููุฑูุญูููุฉู ุงูููู ููุจูุฑูููุงุชูู*
*๏บู๏บดููููููููููููููู๏ปขู ๏บ๏ป๏ป๏ปชู ๏บ๏ป๏บฎูู๏บฃู๏ปคู๏ปฆู ู๏บ๏ป๏บฎูู๏บฃู๏ปดูููููู๏ปข*

๐ *INTISARI KHUTBAH JUMAAT JDT* ๐
๐ *TARIKH : 29 SYAABAN 1443H/ 1 APRIL 2022*

๐ *_TAJUK:  RAMADHAN YANG DINANTI_*

Firman Allah SWT di dalam Surah Al Baqarah ayat 185 yang bermaksud: โ(Masa yang diwajibkan kamu berpuasa itu ialah) bulan Ramadan yang padanya diturunkan Al-Quran, menjadi petunjuk bagi sekalian manusia, dan menjadi keterangan-keterangan yang menjelaskan petunjuk dan (menjelaskan) perbezaan antara yang benar dengan yang salah. Oleh itu, sesiapa dari antara kamu yang menyaksikan anak bulan Ramadan (atau mengetahuinya), maka hendaklah ia berpuasa bulan itu"

๐ 1. Bertaqwa kepada Allah SWT.

๐ 2.  Beberapa hari lagi kita bakal menyambut ketibaan bulan Ramadhan yang penuh dengan kemuliaan, kerahmatan dan keberkatan. Bulan yang diturunkan Al-Quran dan dijanjikan dengan rahmat pada awal kedatangan, diikuti dengan pengampunan dosa pada pertengahan dan dibebaskan dari api neraka pada hujungnya. Dan adanya malam lailatul qadar.

๐ 3.   Bulan Ramadhan adalah waktu terbaik untuk kita mendidik diri ke arah kebaikan yang mana kita bukan sahaja diwajibkan untuk berpuasa dan mengawal hawa nafsu, bahkan kita dituntut untuk memperbanyakkan amal ibadah. Bagi hamba Allah yang benar-benar menghidupkan bulan Ramadhan akan digandakan pahala, dimakbulkan doa, diampunkan dosa, dibuka seluasnya pintu syurga dan ditutup pintu neraka serta syaitan akan dibelenggu.

๐ 4.   Kita perlu mempersiapkan diri untuk menyambut bulan Ramadhan dan berusaha menghidupkannya dengan amalan-amalan yang dapat mendekatkan diri kita kepada Allah SAW. Berdoa agar diberikan umur yang panjang dan kesihatan yang terbaik untuk beribadah sepanjang bulan Ramadhan. Melakukan persediaan jasmani kerana anggota yang sihat akan memudahkan seseorang untuk beribadah.
 
๐ 5.  Persiapan rohani juga perlu bagi meningkatkan keimanan kita kepada Allah SAW. Kita hendaklah sentiasa tunduk dan patuh atas segala perintahnya dan yakin akan ganjaran dan kebaikan yang akan diperoleh pada sepanjang bulan Ramadhan. 

๐ 6.    Kita juga perlu mempelajari dan mengulangkaji ilmu tentang ibadah puasa bagi memastikan ibadah yang kita lakukan diterima Allah SAW dan seterusnya memberi kesan yang baik kepada diri kita. Hendaklah kita berazam untuk meninggalkan dosa dan perbuatan yang buruk dengan bertaubat dari segala dosa kerana Ramadhan adalah bulan penyucian jiwa dan penghapus dosa.

๐ 7.    Persiapan kewangan juga perlu diambil kira kerana amat digalakkan untuk melakukan amalan bersedekah jariah seperti amalan memberi makan kepada orang yang berpuasa.

๐ 8.   Rumusannya, sempena kedatangan Ramadhan ini, marilah kita memanfaatkan dan mengambil peluang serta berusaha menghidupkan bulan Ramadhan dengan melakukan seberapa banyak amal ibadah. Jadikan Ramadhan kali ini sebagai bulan untuk kita melipatgandakan amalan bagi memperoleh ganjaran dan pahala yang besar di sisi Allah SWT. Semoga bulan Ramadhan ini membawa perubahan yang besar dalam diri kita agar menjadi hamba yang bertaqwa di sisi Allah SAW.

Waallahua'lam.

*#Disediakan oleh Unit Khutbah & Tafsir, PMS-JAINJ*

[10/04/2022, 6:04:34โฏPM] ~โฏMohammed: โThis message was deleted.
[10/04/2022, 6:30:41โฏPM] ุนุจุฏุงููู ุงููุธุงุฑู: [TEACHING AND LEARNING METHOD (TnL) OF SCHOOL OF COMPUTING]

โุงูุณูููุงููู ุนููููููููู ููุฑูุญูููุฉู ุงูููู ููุจูุฑูููุงุชููู, ไฝๅฅฝ, เฎตเฎฃเฎเฏเฎเฎฎเฏ,
Greetings to all UTMians,

Referring to the matter above, a meeting was held on 10 April 2022, Sunday regarding the teaching and learning (TnL)  methods.The following is the outcome of the meeting :

1. The TnL methods for School of Computing are based on the Academic Circular issued on 31st January 2022.

2. For Part 1, which is from 20th and 21st Mar 2022 until 28th and 29th April 2022, the TnL methods are based on the Academic Circular No. 01/2022 : Teaching And Learning Methods During Pandemic on 24th January 2022.

3. For Part 2, which is from 8th and 9th May 2022 until 30th June 2022 and 1st July 2022, the TnL methods are based on  Academic Circular No. 02/2022 : Teaching And Learning Implementation Method for Endemic Transition Phase Semester ll Session 2021/2022. For courses that are carried out via online will remain without any changes, meanwhile students may decide to attend the TnL activities online or face-to-face for courses that are carried out in a blended manner according to the approval of the course lecturers respectively.

4. The implementation of summative assessment for the final examination will be subjected to the discretion of the course lecturers respectively. For example, if the lecturer decides to carry out face-to-face assessment, students will need to ensure that they are on campus before the final exam is conducted physically.

Thank you.

SC: Student Representative Council
Universiti Teknologi Malaysia
Session 2021/2022

[11/04/2022, 6:27:55โฏPM] Haitham Al-Sharee UTM: Requirements Documents For open bank account at *RHB Tun Aminah*.

1. Approval letter from emgs. 
2. Letter from utm. 
Link for 1 and 2 : 
https://docs.google.com/forms/d/e/1FAIpQLSec5ZHcR2f0LmStwRsOspp8dx1nz0Uv8MPoRPlTR1pEaOkd7A/viewform

3. Malaysia hand phone bill or any proof that is your number. 
4. Original passport.
5. Copy of passport( details page only).
6. Copy of your visa.
7. Copy of your matric card.
8. If you are renting a house Copy of your rental. agreement or payment receipt. If you are renting a room Copy of electricity bill or water bill.
9. Bank statement of your Father or your sponsor.
10. Deposit  RM1000. You can withdraw it after 2 days.

Finally send all this documents to madam Tiang Shee Hoon on WhatsApp and get your appointment

We are happy to share that the *James Dyson Award 2022* is now open for entries.

The James Dyson Award is an annual international design competition and is accepting submission from young inventors. This yearโs National Winners, to be announced in Sept, will receive ยฃ5,000 (RM27,900) to support the development of their invention. The prize monies for national winners have more than double from previous years.

๐ Winners can expect:
- Money Prize
- Media Attention
- Past Winner Support

The competition accepts individual and team submissions (up to 10 pax) from current students in university or recent graduates in the last four years from design or engineering disciplines.
